msg:Facilities: The facilities are complete and meet the standards of Marriott. The curtain of the bathtub is fun and can be opened and closed back and forth. It is very comfortable to take a bath and look out the window. The curtains slowly opened when entering the door, and the Huangpu River was in front of me. I was very happy to stay in such an expensive hotel for the first time with my father and children. Although it has been raining, the Huangpu River at night has a unique beauty. The money is worth it.
Hygiene: The hygiene is OK, it is quite clean and tidy, the bedding is also cleaned neatly, and the toilet is relatively clean and refreshing. You can stay at ease.
Environment: Located in Pudong New Area, you need to cross the river. I took a taxi directly here, so it feels pretty good. It is not very close to the subway station, but it is no problem for young people. Older people can take a taxi. There is a fountain outside the hotel, and it has all the qualities that a light luxury five-star hotel should have.
Service: The service attitude of the staff is very good. The front desk lady is beautiful and looks comfortable and gentle. I don't know if all girls in Jiangnan area are like this. I waited for more than half an hour to check in, but there was communication and follow-up at any time. I didn't ignore it. I felt respected. It was very good. The front desk brother of the swimming room spoke English very well. I can't help but feel ashamed. Haha, the child swam with his father twice. It was a paradise for children. The overall feeling was good. The breakfast was also great. Maybe it was the first time I stayed in such an expensive hotel. I felt very good. I was full and embarrassed. Hahaha, I ate a lot of smoked salmon. Auntie Xiao wonton made and cooked it now. The variety of bread, western pastries and Chinese food was OK. My dad also said that although it was a bit expensive, it was still worth it. As long as the family liked it, we had a wonderful night.
